OPERATIONS BASIS PRESENTATION Sunbeam Corporation (the "Company") leading designer, manufacturer, marketer consumer branded products. The Sunbeam/registered trademark/ Oster/registered trademark/ brands household names generations, Company market share leader product categories. The Company markets products virtually category retailer including mass merchandisers, catalog showrooms, warehouse clubs, department stores, catalogs, Company-owned outlet stores, television shopping channels, hardware stores, home centers, drug grocery stores, pet supply retailers, independent distributors military. The Company sells products commercial end-users hotels institutions. As Note 2, March 30, 1998, wholly owned subsidiary Company acquired CLN Holdings, Inc. ("CLN Holdings"). As result acquisition CLN Holdings, Company indirect owner approximately 80.9% total number outstanding shares The Coleman Company, Inc. ("Coleman"). Coleman leading manufacturer marketer consumer products worldwide outdoor recreation market. Its products sold domestically internationally Coleman/registered trademark/ brand 1920's. To standardize fiscal period ends Sunbeam recent acquisitions Note 2, Company changed fiscal year-end Sunday nearest December 31 December 31, effective 1998 fiscal year. Accordingly, quarter 1998 period-end changed March 29 March 31. The impact change net sales quarter 1998 approximately $5 million (excluding impact Coleman acquired March 30). This change fiscal year-end puts Sunbeam recent acquisitions fiscal reporting basis. In opinion management, unaudited condensed consolidated financial statements furnished include adjustments (consisting recurring adjustments exception extraordinary charge 1998 loss discontinued operations 1997) fair presentation results operations interim periods presented. RESULTS Revenues quarter 1998 $244.3 million, compared $253.5 million quarter 1997. Before one-time charges $36.8 million early retirement debt compensation expense relating three-year employment agreements Sunbeam's top executives, net loss continuing operations $7.8 million 1998 quarter versus net income continuing operations $20.6 million year-ago quarter. After one-time charges $.43 share, loss share $0.52 1998 quarter compared earnings share $0.08 1997 period. Domestic sales, representing 74% total revenues (excluding Coleman) 1998 quarter, declined 15.4% 1997 quarter due lower price realization unit volume declines. Most domestic sales decline outdoor cooking products due lower anticipated retail sell- products. International sales, representing 26% total revenues quarter, grew 14.0% quarter 1997. This sales growth driven primarily improved distribution product sales Latin America, partially offset lower sales outdoor cooking products Europe Canada. The gross margin quarter 1998 decreased 13.3 percentage points 13.4%, primarily due margin erosion appliance, health home <PAGE> 2 outdoor cooking categories. <PAGE> 3 EARNINGS EXPECTATIONS Based growth restructuring initiatives announced today, including anticipated synergies cost savings, Sunbeam expects full-year 1998 earnings range approximately $1.00 share, excluding one-time costs integrate Coleman, First Alert Signature Brands Sunbeam close Sunbeam's Mexican facilities. These one-time costs expected total approximately $280 million pre-tax, including cash costs approximately $150 million pre-tax. Sunbeam expects extraordinary cash charge approximately $100 million pre-tax quarter 1998 early retirement existing Coleman debt. Based growth restructuring initiatives, including anticipated synergies cost savings, Sunbeam expects 1999 earnings range approximately $2.00 share. From 1999 base, Sunbeam's goal earnings share growth future years range 15-20%.
